 tippaniyan As per the decisions taken by the Railways to prevent the misuse of its website, only two tickets a day (from 8 am to 10 pm) are valid on IRCTC with a user ID, while in Tatkal booking also from 10 am to 12 pm

 Union Minister of State for Labor Oscar Fernandes has resigned from the post of minister to contribute to the Congress party in the next Lok Sabha elections
 furnandis mantri pad ke saath-saath congress ke mahasachiv pad kii jimmevary bhi sambhaal rahe the
